```

For first RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the third parameter is null that violated the required predicate `randomized[random]`. Null is acceptable that a default secure implemetation (`new SecureRandom()`) will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#211.

For second RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the second parameter is custom TrustManager that violated `generatedTrustManagers[tm]`. The predicate requires that the TrustManager must be generated from `TrustManagerFactory.getTrustManagers()`, however, developer can implement custom TrustManager.

For third RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the first parameter is null that violated the required predicate `generatedKeyManagers[km]`. Null is accpetable that a default secure implemetation will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#122.

```

For first RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the third parameter is null that violated the required predicate `randomized[random]`. Null is acceptable that a default secure implemetation (`new SecureRandom()`) will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#211.

For second RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the second parameter is custom TrustManager that violated `generatedTrustManagers[tm]`. The predicate requires that the TrustManager must be generated from `TrustManagerFactory.getTrustManagers()`, however, developer can implement custom TrustManager.

For third RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the first parameter is null that violated the required predicate `generatedKeyManagers[km]`. Null is accpetable that a default secure implemetation will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#122.

For first RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the third parameter is null that violated the required predicate `randomized[random]`. Null is acceptable that a default secure implemetation (`new SecureRandom()`) will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#211.

For second RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the second parameter is custom TrustManager that violated `generatedTrustManagers[tm]`. The predicate requires that the TrustManager must be generated from `TrustManagerFactory.getTrustManagers()`, however, developer can implement custom TrustManager.

For third RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the first parameter is null that violated the required predicate `generatedKeyManagers[km]`. Null is accpetable that a default secure implemetation will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#122.

For ConstraintError, ITP: The rule in `javax.net.ssl.SSLContext` miss valid parameter value `TLS` in Android.

For first RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the third parameter is null that violated the required predicate `randomized[random]`. Null is acceptable that a default secure implemetation (`new SecureRandom()`) will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#211.

For second RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the second parameter is custom TrustManager that violated `generatedTrustManagers[tm]`. The predicate requires that the TrustManager must be generated from `TrustManagerFactory.getTrustManagers()`, however, developer can implement custom TrustManager.

For third RequiredPredicateError, ITP: the first parameter is null that violated the required predicate `generatedKeyManagers[km]`. Null is accpetable that a default secure implemetation will be used. pls refer to https://developer.android.com/reference/javax/net/ssl/SSLContext#init(javax.net.ssl.KeyManager[],%20javax.net.ssl.TrustManager[],%20java.security.SecureRandom). https://android.googlesource.com/platform/external/conscrypt/+/97e7586/src/main/java/org/conscrypt/SSLParametersImpl.java#122.

For ConstraintError, ITP: The rule in `javax.net.ssl.SSLContext` miss valid parameter value `TLS` in Android.
